 siie chahta he ki obama jab bharat jaaen to ve apni hi car main sawari karen
 So the question is, what is this in Obama's car? Is he more hi-tech and safer than Modi's car? Come, let us know that the 10 features of this car are -1
 windo:obama kii car ke windo glass 5 se 6 inch mote or bamrodhi hai
 It has better visibility glass than the car of former presidents
 sirf driver kii ore vaali windo hi kholi ja sakati he, vah bhi sirf 2
 75 inches
 taaki driver baahar maujuud sikret sarvice agent se baat kar sake
 2
 daravaaje:aath inch mote daravaajon kaa vajan bowing 757 vimaan ke daravaajon ke vajan ke baraabar he
 This weight is due to those layers of steel that make the car bulletproof
 3
 Passenger section: a combination of both security and luxury can be seen in the car where Obama and his guests sit
 yahaan chaar log baith sakate hai
 This section also has a glass partition, which the President can open
 iske alaava koi khatra hone par raashtrapati ke liye ek painic batan diya gaya he
 The president can stay connected to his office computer only by car
 unke paas sikyord wifai internet conection rahata he
 Apart from this, the car also has a satellite phone, so that the President remains directly connected to the Pentagon and the Vice President
 4
 Interior: The interior of the car is designed in such a way that it is completely sealed in the event of a chemical attack
 iske alaava car kisi khatre kii sthiti main khud ko puri tarah lock kar leti he
 And becomes safe like a bank vault
 5
 Driver: Obama's car driver is not an ordinary driver
 vah special siie agent he
 Which has been given special training for all the situations that can come during driving
 isamen aam masini kharabi se lekar sabhi immergency se nipatna shaamil he

 6

 iske alaava is car main ful ko khaas fom ke saath bharaa jaataa he taaki aag lagane par usamen visphot na ho
 7
 dephence system:sirf james bond hi nahin, obama kii car main bhi aise kai special upkaran he jo hamale kii sthiti main upyogi hai

 yadi kisi vajah se tair kharaab bhi ho jaaen to car kii flats-ran technology kaam aati he

 9

 yah lagati bhi kisi mahajeev kii tarah he

 10

 or kisi bhi tarah car ke bheetar uskaa asar na ho
